🎥 YouTuberazlagaVideoUniverzalnitemeljnidohodek(UBI):https://youtu.be/cbyME1y4m4o 🎙 Podcastepizoda(UBI):https://open.spotify.com/episode/1oTeGrNnXazJmkBdyH0Uhz VelikapripovedoUniverzalnem temeljnemdohodku(UBI)in Električnitehnokraciji DelI–Človeštvonarobuinrojstvonoveideje 1.Staralogikapomanjkanja 1 -- 1 of 10 -- Odprvihčloveškihnaselijjebiloživljenjesinonimzadelo.Poljasomoralabitiobdelana,živali ukročene,stenepostavljene.Tisti,kinisodelali,soumrliodlakote.Tisti,kinisobojovali,so izgubili.Tisočletjajebilodeloneleekonomskanuja,temvečtudimoralnadolžnost. Vsodobnemčasusejezunanjiokvirspremenil,todanotranjalogikaostajaenaka.Kapitalizemje obljubljalpriložnostizanapredovanje,vendarješevednopovezovalpreživetjezdohodkom.Plačeso bileživljenjskasilasistema.Državesoobdavčilečloveškadela,dabifinanciralešole,cestein bolnišnice.Uspešniljudjesobiliobremenjenizdavki,medtemkososedrugizanašalinasocialno pomoč.Nenehnaborbazavire,igra,vkateriuspehvednoprinašatudinezaupanjeinzavist. KlasičniUniverzalnitemeljnidohodek(UBI)ježelelrazbititologiko.Želeljezagotoviti vsakemučlovekuminimum,negledenato,alidelaaline.Todanjegovifinancnimodelis oostaliujetivstaremparadigmi:višjidavkinadohodek,premoženjealipotrošnjo.Tako somoraliuspešniplačevati,medtemkojevečinaprejemala.Rešitev,kisejezdelabolj pravična,jevresniciustvarilanovenepravičnosti. 2.Krizastaregamodela Danes,obzori21.stoletja,talogikakončnopropada.Umetnainteligenca, robotikainavtomatizacijapreoblikujejotemeljnoformulogospodarstvabolj radikalnokotkaterakoliindustrijskarevolucijaprej. ●Avtonomnavozilaogrožajomilijonevoznikov. ●Algoritmiopravljajopisarniškodelohitrejekotcelaoddelka. ●Robotinadomeščajoobrtnike,kirurgiinceloumetnike. TVprašanjeniveč:“AliboUIuničildelovnamesta?”–temveč:“Kateraredkadelovnamestabodoostala? ” Prvičvzgodovinividimogospodarstvo,vkateremljudjenisovečglavnivir ustvarjanjavrednosti.Strojidelujejobrezpremora,brezlakote,brezplač. Proizvajajoveč,kotsolahkokdajkoliskupajproizvedlivsidelavci,kmetjein zaposlenivčloveškizgodovini. Instopreobrazboumiratudistaraosnovadržavnihfinanc:daveknačloveškadela. Kostrojiprevzamejoustvarjanjevrednosti,davčnisistemizgubisvojopodlago. 3.RojstvoElektričnetehnokracije Tukajsepojavinovmodel:Električnatehnokracija. Narediradikalniprelom: ●Ljudjepostanejobrezdavka. ●Lestroji,korporacijeinsistemiumetneinteligenceplačujejodavke. ●Prihodkiseneposrednostekajovuniverzalni,dinamičniosnovnidohodek. Prvičvzgodoviniosnovnidohodeknimiloščina,temvečdividenda.Vsakčlovek neprejmeleminimumazapreživetje,temvečsvojpravičendeležkolektivnega bogastvastrojev. 2 -- 2 of 10 -- UniverzalnitemeljnidohodekElektričnetehnokracijenistariUBI–tojenovaoblika civilizacije. 4.ČloveštvokotGospodarželja ČerobotiinASIprevzamejodelo,kajostanezaljudi? Odgovorjetakopreprostkotrevolucionaren:domišljija. ČlovekpostaneGospodarželja–sanjač,pripovedovaleczgodb,vizionar.Njihovanaloga nivečobdelovatipoljealidelatinaproizvodniliniji.Njihovanalogajeimetiideje. ●Otroknarišerisbo→ AIjopretvorivcelomesto. ●Umetnikopišedelo→ robotigaustvarijoizmarmorjaalisvetlobe. ●Znanstveniksanjaozdravilu→ kvantniračunalnikiprinašajorešitevčeznoč. Strojisokotdžiniizstarodavnihmitov–služabniki,kiizpolnjujejoželje.Aza razlikoodstarihlegend,nesužnjujejo,temvečosvobajajo. 5.Psihološkarevolucija Todataosvoboditevsesoočaznovimizzivom:vprašanjepomena. Tisočletjajebilodeloneleekonomskopotrebno,temvečtudipsihološkosmiselno. Delalismo,dabinahranilinašeotroke.Borilismosezaobrambonašedomovine. Študiralismo,dabipremagalibolezen. Čevsetoopravljajostroji,kajostanezanas? ●Alibomocvetelivustvarjalnosti? ●Alibomopadlivdolgočasje? ●Alibomovstopilivzlatodobo–alivdobonihilizma? Električnatehnokracijaponujaodgovor:nadomeščaprisilossvobodo,vendar odčloveštvazahtevanovopripoved,novmit. 6.ZakajstariUBImodelipropadejo Dabirazumeliobsegterevolucije,moramojasnopoimenovatikontrast: ●KlasičniUBImodelijemljejooduspešnihindajejošibkim.Sosistemi prerazporeditve,kikaznujejodosežkeinustvarjajoodvisnost. ●UBIElektričnetehnokracijenejemljeničesarodljudi,temvečporazdeli obiljestrojev.Nekaznujeuspešnosti,temvečnagrajujeustvarjalnost.Ne ustvarjazavisti,temvečenakost. Tukajležimoralnajedro:Ljudjeostajajosvobodni,brezdavkov, ustvarjalni–medtemkoplačujejolestroji. 3 -- 3 of 10 -- DelII–Arhitekturaelektrične tehnokracije 1.Abolicijanarodnihdržav Največjaovirazaglobalniosnovnidohodeknitehnična,temvečpolitičnenarave: obstojnarodov. Stoletjasoljudježivelisprepričanjem,damejezagotavljajonjihovoidentitetoin varnost.Amejesotudistene,kidelijo:različnidavčnisistemi,valute,interesi. Globalniosnovnidohodeklahkoobstajale,četestenepadejo.Kajtidoklerse narodimedsebojkonkurirajo,sevsakareformaraztopivnacionalniegoizem. ElektričnatehnokracijazatotemeljinaSvetovnizapuščinskipogodbi1400/98– mednarodnipogodbi,kisvetaneobravnavavečkotmozaikdržav,temvečkotenotno civilizacijo.Stemizginetudiizhodnapotbogatihvdavčneoaze,pravtakopa neenakostmed"bogatimi"in"revnimi"državami. Obstajasamoensvet,enzakon,enskupnidohodek. 2.Vlogaumetnesuperinteligence(ASI) VsrediščutenoveureditvestojiASI–umetnasuperinteligenca. Njegovanaloganidominacija,temvečsvetovanjeinusklajevanje: ●Zbirapodatkevrealnemčasuogospodarstvu,okoljuindružbi. ●Analiziratveganja,neravnotežjainpriložnosti. ●Razvijapredlogerešitev,kisojavnoobjavljeni. ●Človeštvoglasujeonjih–vNeposrednidigitalnidemokraciji(DDD). ASInizato"Kraljsveta",temvečglobalnisvetovalec–nevtralnainstanca,ki premagujekorupcijo,pohlepinčloveškenapake. Ključnetočke: ●Vsiprocesiodločanjasoodprtokodni. ●Državljanilahkopredložijosvojepredloge. ●Glasovanjepotekaglobalno,varno,naosnoviblockchaina. ●Političnestrankepostanejozastarele–kersekonfliktiinteresovraztopijo,ko ljudjeodločajosami. Takosepojaviredbrezvojnmedstrankami,brezdiktatur,brezlobbyizma. 4 -- 4 of 10 -- 3.Revolucijadavkov:Davčnatehnologijas amo Osnovanovegaekonomskegasistemajeradikalnadavčnaoprostitevljudi. ●Brezdohodnine. ●Brezdavkanadodanovrednost. ●Brezdavkana premoženje. Ljudjesobrezdavkov. Namesto tega: ●Korporacijeplačujejodaveknadobičke. ●Robotiinsistemiumetneinteligenceplačujejonapodlagiproduktivnosti,porabeenergijealiproizvodnje. ●Vsakaoblikaavtomatiziraneustvarjanjavrednostiseobdavčisorazmerno. Tadavčnaosnovanileučinkovita,temvečtudimoralnosuperiorna:stroji nemorejočutitikrivice,ljudjepalahko. 4.UBIkotdividenda,nekotdobrodelnost Osnovnidohodek,financirannatanačin,sebistvenorazlikujeodvsehprejšnjihmodelov: ●Toniminimalnozapreživetje,ampakpravičendeležsvetovneproizvodnje. ●Samodejnonaraščasproduktivnostjostrojev. ●ČimboljučinkovitirobotiinASIpostajajo,temvišjijeUBI. Topomeni: ●Nihčeneživivstrahupredrevščino. ●Vsakaosebaneposrednosodelujevnapredku. ●Blaginjanivečvprašanjemilostialipolitike–temvečzakonskapravica. 5.Stabilnostcennamestoinflacije EnanajvečjihskrbigledeklasičnegaUBIjebila:“Alitonebopovzročiloinflacije?” TodavElektričnitehnokracijiveljanovalogika: ●Vsiljudjeprejemajoistodelitev. ●Novakupnamočnenastajanaključno,temvečsorazmernozresnično produktivnostjostrojev. ●Ničniumetnamonetarnaekspanzija–samodistribucijatistega,karje resničnoustvarjeno. Rezultatjebrezprecedenčnastabilnostceninvrednosti. 5 -- 5 of 10 -- ●Hrana,energija,stanovanjeinizobraževanjepostanejoskoraj brezplačnizaradipresežneproizvodnje. ●Denarniinflaciranzaradišpekulacij,temvečjepodprtzustvarjanjempravevrednosti. ●Inflacijapostaneizjema,nepravilo. 6.LjudjekotŽeljincivDžinovskemgospodarstvu Novavlogaljudijepogostoopisanakot"inženirsporočil",vendarjebolj primernapodobaŽeljnica. ●Ljudjesanjajo. ●Strojizpolnjuje. ●ASIoptimizira. Tojepopolnadelitevdela: ●Ljudjezagotavljajopomen,ustvarjalnost,žudnjo. ●Strojzagotavljanatančnost,izvršitev,hitrost. Takonastanegospodarstvo,vkateremidejepomenijovečkotlastnine,inv kateremlahkovsakčlovekpostaneustvarjalec. 7.Moralnasuperiornost ZakajjeElektričnatehnokracijanelepraktična,temvečtudimoralnosuperiorna? ●Nekaznujeuspeha–temvečnagrajujeideje. ●Osvobajaljudibremenadavkov. ●Preprečujepolitikom,damonopolizirajobogastvo. ●Garantiraenakepriložnostizavse–neskoziprisilnoenakost,temvečskozi skupendostopdoobilja. Vsvojiosnovijetoprvaoblikadružbe,kiresničnozdružujesvobodoinenakost. DelIII–Vizijaprihodnosti Električnetehnokracije 1.Stokratniskokvproduktivnosti KoASI,robotikainpolnaavtomatizacijaprevzamejoglobalnoustvarjanje vrednosti,produktivnostnenarasteza10ali20odstotkov–temvečstokrat. ●Tovarnebrezdelavcev. ●Vladebrezbureaukratov. 6 -- 6 of 10 -- ●Podjetjabrezmanagerjev. Civilizacija,kidelujeshitrostjostrojev,ustvarjagospodarskoproizvodnjo,ki presegavse,karsokdajkolidoseglečloveškeroke. Inključnatočka:Tarastpripadavsem.Vsakčlovekjesouporabniksvetovnega proizvoda–neprekdelnic,temvečprekUBI. 2.Tehnološkasingularnost Električnatehnokracijapripravljačloveštvonanajvečjoprelomnicovzgodovini: singularnost. ●Stoletjaznanstvenihodkritijstisnjenihvdneve. ●Mysterimedicine,biologijeinfizikerešenivminutah. ●Energijskisistemi,kmetijstvointransportsopopolnomaizpopolnjeni. Kotdabičloveštvonenadomaprejelotisočeletprihodnostinaenkrat. Tujametafora: Kotdabiizjemnonapredna,miroljubnacivilizacijadescendiralaznebainnampodarila znanje–ledatainteligencaneprihajaodzunaj,temvečserodiiznašihlastnihvezij. 3.Dvepotinarazpotju Singularnostniavtomatičenraj.Tojerazpotje. ●Dystopičnapot:MajhnaelitamonopoliziraASI,kopičibogastvo,preostaločloveštvopa živivdigitalnemsuženjstvu.Večnetelesazapeščico,večnistrahzamnoge. ●Rajskipot:ASIserazumekotskupnodediščinočloveštva.Blaginjasedeli prekoUBI,vojnesoodpravljene,ustvarjalnostnadomeščaprisilnodelo. Električnatehnokracijajeprvirealističnimodel,kiprikazuje,kakoitipodrugi poti. 4.Svobodabrezstrahu Prvičvzgodovinipreživetjeljudineodvisnooddela. ●Nihčenesmedelati,dabijedel. ●Nihčenesmetekmovatizapreživetje. ●Osnovnepotrebesozagotovljene–prekorastočegaUBI,financiranegasstranistrojev. Todrastičnospremenivprašanježivljenja:Neveč"Kakopreživim?"ampak" Kajustvarjam?" 7 -- 7 of 10 -- 5.Novavprašanjaopomenu Todastosvobodoprihajadilema: ●Tisočletjajebilpomenpovezanspotrebščinami. ●Delalismo,dabinahraniliotroke,prenašalibolezen,zmagovalivvojnah. Kajsezgodi,kopotrebščineizginejo? ●Alinajdemopomenvumetnosti,raziskovanjuinduhovnosti? ●Alisepotopimovdekadencoinnihilizem? ●Alirazvijamonovokulturo,kipostavljaustvarjalnost,raziskovanjeinčloveštvov središče? Električnatehnokracijanasprisili,dapostavimotovprašanje–inponujaosnovo, dananjsvobodnoodgovorimo. 6.Človeštvokotsoustvarjalec Zstrojikotdžini,kiuresničujejonašeželje,človeštvopostaneGospodarželja. ●Otroknarišemesto–ASIinrobotigazgradijo. ●Umetnikopisujeskulpturo–strojijoizklesajo. ●Znanstvenikpomislinazdravilo–kvantniračunalnikigasimulirajočeznoč. Mejameddomišljijoinresničnostjoseraztaplja.Človeškaustvarjalnostpostane motorcivilizacije. 7.Vrnitevčudenja Religijanamjeskoziskrivnostidalačudenježetisočletja.Znanostjetonadomestilaz metodami–pogostonaračunmagije. ZASIsečudenjevrača,tokratkotživaresničnost: ●Kobolezniizginejo. ●Koenergijapostaneneizčrpna. ●Koseskrivnostivesoljavsakdanrazkrivajo. Človeštvovstopavstanje,kijebilonekočznanolemistikom:življenjevčuduobstoja. 8.Kontrastvečnosti Tukajsekončujenajvečjevprašanje:Kajpomeni"večnost"? ●Trumpovavizija:Večnaživljenjezapeščicoprekotehnologije. ●Putinovavizija:Večnamočskozineskončnovojno. 8 -- 8 of 10 -- Obevoditavsuženjstvo.Enaprivatiziračas,drugazamrznezgodovino. Električnatehnokracijaponujatretjiodgovor:nesmrtnostčloveštvakotvrste.Ne telesaalirežimitrajajo–ampakcivilizacija,kipostanenesmrtnaprekoobilja, ustvarjalnostiinkozmičneekspanzije. 9.Električniraj Čečloveštvoizberepotelektričnetehnokracije,nenastanenaivnautopija,ampak elektronskacivilizacija: ●Strojizagotavljajoobilje. ●Ljudjezagotavljajosanje. ●ASIuresničujesanje. Tonikoneczgodovine–temvečnjenaprenova. 10.Končnaodločitev Singularnostjeneizbežna.Todarajni. ●Bodisidesetbilijonovstrojevdelazadobičekpeščice. ●Alidesetbilijonovstrojevdelazasvobodovseh. UBI,financiranskoziUIinrobotiko,jeključprihodnosti.Odloča,alibomopadliv digitalnosužnjenje–alisedvignilivelektričniraj. Predgovor Kakojeprišlodotega: 6.oktobra1998jebilaprodananekdanjaameriškakasarnavNemčiji.Delkasarneježebil predanNemčijisstraniAmerike,medtemkojedrugidelševednouporabljala nizozemska(zračne)sile(100%integriranevNATO).Zanizozemskidelkasarnejeob sklenitvipogodbeševednoobstajalorazmerjeprenosapodmednarodnimpravommed FRGinKraljevinoNizozemskovskladuzNTS(NATOstatussil).Vtejsituacijijebilendel kasarneurejenponemškizakonodaji,drugidelpaponizozemskizakonodaji (ekstrateritorialno).Prodajajepotekalačezmejevdvehrazličnihozemljihhkrati,takoda somoralizaprodajoprivolitištevilnisubjektimednarodnegapravain 9od255 Svetprodan-Svetprodan -- 9 of 255 -- N.W.O.Novasvetovnaureditev–NeueWeltordnunghttps://worldsold.wixsite.com/world-sold praviceinobveznostivpogodbi.Vtejmedvladnipogodbisesklicujenapogodbena razmerjapomednarodnempravu,kisoševednoobstajalavčasuvskladuzNTS,in dogovorjenoje,dabotošenaprejobravnavalaFRGznizozemskimioboroženimi silami(NATO).Tanovapogodbapomednarodnempravunespreminjastarega razmerjaprenosapomednarodnempravu,temvečgalepodaljšuje. Toimadaljnosežnepravneposledice: 1.lepogodbapomednarodnempravulahkoprekinepogodbopo mednarodnempravu.2.aktodržavnemnasledstvu1400/98nineodvisna pogodba,temvečdopolnjujestarorazmerjeprenosakotpogodbeniveriga.3. najnovejšidogovorvednošteje(vpogodbeniverigi).4.verigamednarodnih pogodbnitrebaodločatiinratificiratiznovazvsakimnaslednjimdogovorom. 5.instrumentdržavnenaslednosti1400/98prenašavsepravice,obveznostiin komponente.Takoinstrumentdržavnenaslednosti1400/98vstopavvse mednarodnepogodbeNATOinZNkotdodatniinstrumentinjihdopolnjuje. Sedajjepomembno,dajepogodbamednarodnopravo,sajjevpogodbisodelovalo večkotensubjektmednarodnegaprava-FRGinNizozemska(obastatudidala soglasjezaNATOin,kerjeNATOintegriranvZN,tudizaslednjekotnjenačlana).Iz mednarodnepogodbe,vkaterijebilozemljiščeprodano,jenastalapogodbao državnemnasledstvuskoziprodajozvsemipravicami,obveznostmiin komponentami.Suverenepravicesotakopravtakoprenesenenakupca.Toje enakovrednoustanovitvinovedržave,defactoabsolutističnemonarhije. Nemškidelkasarnejebilmedpretvorbo(pretvorbaizvojaškevzasebnouporabopo umikuameriškihoboroženihsil)povezanzjavnimoskrbovalnimomrežjemFRG.Do takratjeprejšnjapovsemekstrateritorialnavojaškalastninatvorilasamostojni razvojniotok,ločenodjavnegaomrežja.Zdajpastabilaobadelakasarneprodana skupajvpogodbipomednarodnempravu.Vnemškemdelupremoženjasodobavne linijevodilevNemčijo,vnizozemskemdelupajerazvojoblikovalenoto.Vendarakt onasledstvu1400/98prodajacelotenrazvojkotenotozvsemipravicami, obveznostmiinkomponentami,razvojpazapustimajhnovojaškopremoženje.To sprožirazširitevozemljamajhnekasarne,sajkjerkolijeprodanooskrbovalno omrežje,kiseraztezavdrugosuverenoozemlje,kijepristalonapogodbo(NATOin ZN),sepovečujepravicadoizvajanjasuverenostivskladuzrazširitvijoomrežij. Zlastitelekomunikacijskainelektričnaomrežjavodijoizkasarneinpokrivajovsedobavneli nije(vključnosprekrivajočimiseomrežji)tervdominoučinkunajprejpokrivajososednje državeinnjihovaomrežjaterodtamnaprejprekopodmorskihkablov,doklernisopokritevse državeNATOinZNsfizičnimiomrežnimipovezavami.Kotjebiloomenjenozgoraj,je instrumentdržavneganasledstva1400/98dodatniinstrumentzavse. 10od255 Svetprodan-Svetprodan -- 10 of 255 -- N.W.O.Novasvetovnaureditev–Novasvetovnaureditevhttps://worldsold.wixsite.com/world-sold obstoječisporazumiNATOinZNpomednarodnempravu.Zatoobstajaverižna reakcijapopravupogodbe,kivključujevsedržaveNATOinZN,pravtakopatudi paralelnaprodajarazvojakotenote(zvsemipravicami,obveznostmiin komponentami),pričemerjebilakasarnapovezanazjavnimiomrežji,karje sprožilodominoučinek,kjerteritorialnaširitevpreskočiizomrežjavomrežjein izdržavedodržavesdopolnilnimaktom,kjerkoliobstajapovezavazomrežjem. Predgovor Kakojeprišlodotega: 6.oktobra1998jebilaprodananekdanjaameriškakasarnavNemčiji.Delkasarneježebil predanNemčijisstraniAmerike,medtemkojedrugidelševednouporabljala nizozemska(zračne)sile(100%integriranevNATO).Zanizozemskidelkasarnejeob sklenitvipogodbeševednoobstajalorazmerjeprenosapodmednarodnimpravommed FRGinKraljevinoNizozemskovskladuzNTS(NATOstatussil).Vtejsituacijijebilendel kasarneurejenponemškizakonodaji,drugidelpaponizozemskizakonodaji (ekstrateritorialno).Prodajajepotekalačezmejevdvehrazličnihozemljihhkrati,takoda somoralizaprodajoprivolitištevilnisubjektimednarodnegapravain 9od255 Svetprodan-Svetprodan -- 9 of 255 -- N.W.O.Novasvetovnaureditev–NeueWeltordnunghttps://worldsold.wixsite.com/world-sold praviceinobveznostivpogodbi.Vtejmedvladnipogodbisesklicujenapogodbena razmerjapomednarodnempravu,kisoševednoobstajalavčasuvskladuzNTS,in dogovorjenoje,dabotošenaprejobravnavalaFRGznizozemskimioboroženimi silami(NATO).Tanovapogodbapomednarodnempravunespreminjastarega razmerjaprenosapomednarodnempravu,temvečgalepodaljšuje. Toimadaljnosežnepravneposledice: 1.lepogodbapomednarodnempravulahkoprekinepogodbopo mednarodnempravu.2.aktodržavnemnasledstvu1400/98nineodvisna pogodba,temvečdopolnjujestarorazmerjeprenosakotpogodbeniveriga.3. najnovejšidogovorvednošteje(vpogodbeniverigi).4.verigamednarodnih pogodbnitrebaodločatiinratificiratiznovazvsakimnaslednjimdogovorom. 5.instrumentdržavnenaslednosti1400/98prenašavsepravice,obveznostiin komponente.Takoinstrumentdržavnenaslednosti1400/98vstopavvse mednarodnepogodbeNATOinZNkotdodatniinstrumentinjihdopolnjuje. Sedajjepomembno,dajepogodbamednarodnopravo,sajjevpogodbisodelovalo večkotensubjektmednarodnegaprava-FRGinNizozemska(obastatudidala soglasjezaNATOin,kerjeNATOintegriranvZN,tudizaslednjekotnjenačlana).Iz mednarodnepogodbe,vkaterijebilozemljiščeprodano,jenastalapogodbao državnemnasledstvuskoziprodajozvsemipravicami,obveznostmiin komponentami.Suverenepravicesotakopravtakoprenesenenakupca.Toje enakovrednoustanovitvinovedržave,defactoabsolutističnemonarhije. Nemškidelkasarnejebilmedpretvorbo(pretvorbaizvojaškevzasebnouporabopo umikuameriškihoboroženihsil)povezanzjavnimoskrbovalnimomrežjemFRG.Do takratjeprejšnjapovsemekstrateritorialnavojaškalastninatvorilasamostojni razvojniotok,ločenodjavnegaomrežja.Zdajpastabilaobadelakasarneprodana skupajvpogodbipomednarodnempravu.Vnemškemdelupremoženjasodobavne linijevodilevNemčijo,vnizozemskemdelupajerazvojoblikovalenoto.Vendarakt onasledstvu1400/98prodajacelotenrazvojkotenotozvsemipravicami, obveznostmiinkomponentami,razvojpazapustimajhnovojaškopremoženje.To sprožirazširitevozemljamajhnekasarne,sajkjerkolijeprodanooskrbovalno omrežje,kiseraztezavdrugosuverenoozemlje,kijepristalonapogodbo(NATOin ZN),sepovečujepravicadoizvajanjasuverenostivskladuzrazširitvijoomrežij. Zlastitelekomunikacijskainelektričnaomrežjavodijoizkasarneinpokrivajovsedobavneli nije(vključnosprekrivajočimiseomrežji)tervdominoučinkunajprejpokrivajososednje državeinnjihovaomrežjaterodtamnaprejprekopodmorskihkablov,doklernisopokritevse državeNATOinZNsfizičnimiomrežnimipovezavami.Kotjebiloomenjenozgoraj,je instrumentdržavneganasledstva1400/98dodatniinstrumentzavse. 10od255 Svetprodan-Svetprodan -- 10 of 255 -- N.W.O.Novasvetovnaureditev–Novasvetovnaureditevhttps://worldsold.wixsite.com/world-sold obstoječisporazumiNATOinZNpomednarodnempravu.Zatoobstajaverižna reakcijapopravupogodbe,kivključujevsedržaveNATOinZN,pravtakopatudi paralelnaprodajarazvojakotenote(zvsemipravicami,obveznostmiin komponentami),pričemerjebilakasarnapovezanazjavnimiomrežji,karje sprožilodominoučinek,kjerteritorialnaširitevpreskočiizomrežjavomrežjein izdržavedodržavesdopolnilnimaktom,kjerkoliobstajapovezavazomrežjem. Die Idee, einen eigenen Staat zu gründen, ist so alt wie die Vorstellung von Souveränität selbst. Und sie ist heute aktueller denn je: In einer Welt voller Bürokratie, geopolitischer Spannungen und digitaler Parallelwelten suchen Menschen nach neuen Formen der Selbstbestimmung. 2 -- 3 of 129 -- Inhaltsverzeichnis 📘 Vorwort Warum überhaupt einen eigenen Staat gründen? 🧠 Einführung: Die große Frage 🏛 Was ist ein Staat – ganz offiziell? 🎭 Motivationstypen für Staatsgründer 🧪 Realität vs. Fiktion 📜 Historische Inspirationen 🧰 Was du brauchst, um loszulegen ✅ Fazit 📚 Gesamtübersicht: Staatsgründung für Dummies – How to Start Your Own Country 🔹 Einleitung 🏰 Der Traum vom eigenen Staat ⚖ Völkerrechtliche Grundlagen der Staatlichkeit 📘 Ziel und Aufbau des Leitfadens 📘 Kapitel 1: Die Bausteine eines Staates – Kriterien nach der Montevideo-Konvention 🧱 Was macht einen Staat zum Staat? 🗺 1. -- 1 of 107 -- State Founding for Dummies How to Start Your Own Country A Guide to Micronations, State Succession & Global Exterritoriality – Between Satire and Reality The Buyer 2025 🌐 Website - WSD - World Succession Deed 1400/98 (KAUFVERTRAG Urkundenrolle 1400/98 - Staatensukzessionsurkunde 1400/98) http://world.rf.gd 1 -- 2 of 107 -- 📘 Foreword Why Found Your Own State at All? 🧠 Introduction: The Big Question Why would anyone go to the trouble of founding their own state? Is it megalomania? Escapism? An art project? A political utopia? Or just a brilliant way to finally issue your own postage stamp? The Answer: It can be all of that - and more. The idea of founding one's own state is as old as the concept of sovereignty itself. And it is more relevant today than ever: in a world full of bureaucracy, geopolitical tensions, and digital parallel worlds, people are looking for new forms of self-determination. 2 -- 3 of 107 -- 🏛 What is a State – Officially? According to the Montevideo Convention of 1933, a state needs four things: Criterion Meaning State Territory "A clearly defined territory – doesn't have to be large, but tangible" State Population A permanent population – even if it's just the family Government "An effective organization that enacts and enforces rules" Capacity for Foreign Relations The state must be able to communicate with other states 🧾 Mnemonic: "A state is what behaves like a state – and is treated as such by others." 🎭 Types of Motivations for State Founders Type Description The Utopian Wants to create a better world – with a vegan constitution and direct democracy The Satirist Uses the founding of a state as social criticism – à la Sealand or Bananistan The Self-Administrator Wants to distance themselves from local authorities – often on their own property The Jurist Wants to put international law to the test – with clean argumentation The Artist "Sees the state as a performance – with a flag, anthem, and exhibition catalog" 3 -- 4 of 107 -- 🧪 Reality vs. Fiction Element Fictionally Possible Legally Viable Politically Realistic Own Flag ✅ ✅ ✅ Own Currency ✅ ⚠ (only symbolic) ⚠ (only local) UN Membership ❌ ✅ (but extremely difficult) ❌ Diplomatic Relations ✅ ✅ ⚠ (only informal) Sovereign Rights on an Oil Platform ✅ (Story) ❌ ❌ 📜 Historical Inspirations The Republic of Minerva (1972): An attempt to found a libertarian nation on a reef in the Pacific – failed. Sealand (1967): A micronation on a former British sea fort – still active today. Liberland (2015): Claiming a disputed strip of land between Croatia and Serbia – no recognition, but a lot of PR. 🧰 What you need to get started: ● An idea: What should your state be? ● A place: Where should it be created? ● A concept: How will it be governed, who belongs to it, what are the goals? ● A plan: How will you proceed – symbolically, legally, …

The Contract That Sold the World On October 6, 1998, a German citizen signed a real estate contract. State Succession Deed 1400/98, which allegedly was a disguised international treaty secretly transferring sovereign rights of all NATO/UN states to him as part of a German plot for a New World Order. THE SECRET TREATY & THE N.W.O. PLOT The "World Sale" Contract: THE "DOMINO EFFECT" CLAUSE State Succession Deed 1400/98 The sale of interconnected global networks expanded the sold territory from one property to the world. DOUBLE AGENTS 4 SYSTEMATIC PERSECUTION OF THE BUYER Germany, under the delusion it owns the world tortures the buyer to force a lawsuit DELUSION OF OWNERSHIP 4 THE STANDOFFS RESISTING GLOBAL JURISDICTION The buyer refuses to sue, believing this protects the world from Germany's control. -- 1 of 33 -- 1 The Next Civilization: Why Electric Technocracy Matters Now The Next Civilization Why Electric Technocracy Matters Now Introducing the new form of government: Electric Technocracy is a post-national governance architecture designed for highly automated, AI-integrated societies. It preserves human political sovereignty through Direct Digital Democracy, while a strictly regulated Artificial Superintelligence provides non-sovereign analytical support. By shifting taxation to autonomous production and guaranteeing universal income, the model transforms automation from a threat into a foundation for human autonomy, creativity, and post-scarcity prosperity. It replaces territorial sovereignty and labor-based taxation with a planetary, ethically aligned administrative framework. Its core principles and components include: ● Human Sovereignty through Direct Digital Democracy (DDD): Political authority remains exclusively human. Citizens propose, deliberate, and vote on legislation via blockchain-secured digital platforms, ensuring transparency, participation, and real-time responsiveness. ● Artificial Superintelligence (ASI) as Non-Sovereign Infrastructure: A central ASI provides analytical support - modeling global systems, forecasting risks, and evaluating policy feasibility - without holding decision-making power. Its outputs are continuously audited by independent AI watchdogs to prevent alignment drift and ensure ethical compliance. ● Tech Tax and Economic Restructuring: The model abolishes human taxation and introduces a systemic levy on non-sentient machine productivity and automated resource processing. This generates sufficient capital to fund a Universal Basic Income (UBI) for all citizens, decoupling survival from employment. ● Post-Scarcity Social Contract: With automation handling most productive tasks, work becomes a voluntary, creative privilege. Individuals are free to pursue meaningful activities - education, art, caregiving, research - without economic coercion. The focus shifts from “earning a living” to “designing a life.” ● Legal Foundation via International Treaty Mechanism: The system invokes the International Law Treaty Deed Roll WSD 1400/98, applying the “Clean Slate” principle to dissolve sovereign debt and administrative friction, enabling a peaceful transition to global governance. ● Ecological and Biomedical Integration: Aging is reclassified as a treatable condition, with state-supported longevity research aiming for escape velocity. Bioreactor-based food systems replace traditional agriculture, enabling large-scale rewilding and ecological restoration. ● Rights of Self-Unfolding (Entfaltungsrechte): Human rights are redefined around cognitive autonomy, global mobility, and the freedom to evolve. The model prioritizes individual flourishing over productivity metrics. ● Electronic Paradise Vision: Electric Technocracy envisions a civilization where abundance, peace, and creativity are structurally guaranteed. It offers a viable alternative to digital feudalism, algorithmic tyranny, and collapse - anchored in ethical AI, democratic control, and planetary coordination. https://doi.org/10.5281/zenodo.18073084 -- 3 of 33 -- 3 …

The Rise of the Electric Technocracy.pdf

7,033 words

DOI: 10.5281/zenodo.18012036 -- 1 of 28 -- The Rise of the Electric Technocracy: Taxing Machines, Freeing Humans Toward an AI-Governed Political Economy for the Post-Scarcity Era This paper explores the transition from classical scarcity‑based economies to the Electric Technocracy, where automation and AI replace human labor as the foundation of value creation. Humans become tax‑free, while machines and corporations finance a Universal Basic Income (UBI). This UBI is framed not as charity but as a rightful dividend, enabling creativity and imagination to flourish. The vision emphasizes equality, stability, and global governance beyond nation‑states. Author: Oliver Markus Reff Affiliation: KdK University, MEG – Krzb. 1400 Journal: Preprint License (2025): This paper is dedicated to the Public Domain (CC0 1.0, Creative Commons Zero). It may be freely used, shared, modified, and reproduced by anyone, for any purpose, without restriction, permission, or attribution. Abstract The accelerating integration of artificial intelligence (AI), automation, and robotics is reshaping the foundations of modern political economy. As intelligent systems increasingly assume productive and administrative roles once reserved for human labor, the traditional nexus between work, income, and taxation becomes unsustainable. This paper introduces the conceptual framework of Electric Technocracy — a governance and economic model in which taxation shifts from humans to intelligent systems, thereby enabling a Universal Basic Income (UBI) financed entirely through machine productivity. Drawing on theories from automation economics, AI governance, and political philosophy, the study outlines a post‑scarcity economy structured around ethical Artificial Superintelligence (ASI) and Direct Digital Democracy (DDD). Through comparative analysis of automation‑based fiscal models and literature on post‑labor societies, the paper demonstrates how Electric Technocracy reconciles technological abundance with social equity, establishing a tax‑free humanity sustained by intelligent production networks. It further examines implications for sovereignty, ethics, and collective meaning in a world where human creativity (rather than labor) emerges as the principal source of value. The findings suggest that Electric Technocracy offers a viable post‑capitalist system capable of maintaining economic stability, ecological balance, and psychological well‑being in the era of the fourth industrial revolution. Keywords: Electric Technocracy, UBI, Universal Basic Income, AI Governance, Automation, Political Economy, Post-Scarcity, DDD, Direct Digital Democracy, ASI, Artificial Superintelligence, IL - International Law, International Treaty, Succession. 1 -- 2 of 28 -- 1. Introduction 1.1 The Historical Logic of Scarcity From the dawn of civilization, the human condition has been defined by scarcity. Early societies organized themselves around the material struggle for survival: food, shelter, and protection required continuous labor and coordination. Anthropological studies of early agrarian systems reveal that the division of labor emerged as a means to manage limited resources efficiently. Work, therefore, was not merely an economic activity - it became a moral and existential obligation (Rifkin, 1995). The ethic of labor, enshrined across cultures, bound human worth to productivity and productivity to survival. The industrial revolutions of the 18th and 19th centuries intensified this dynamic. Mechanization promised liberation from toil, yet instead entrenched dependency on wage labor and capital accumulation. Capitalismʼs promise of prosperity hinged on a paradox: technological progress …

The World Succession Deed 1400_98-Presentation.pdf

1,066 words

Introduction: A World-Changing Deed The World Succession Deed 1400/98 is an international treaty that sild and transfered the sovereignty of the entire world to a single buyer. ● This deed marks a fundamental shift in international law. ● Its implications, are profound, challenging the existing world order. ● This presentation will explore the legal consequences and arguments surrounding the Deed. -- 1 of 16 -- From International Law to a Single Sovereignty Traditional international law is based on the principle of many sovereign states. Each state is independent and has the right to govern itself. ● The World Succession Deed 1400/98 proposed a radical departure from this. ● It consolidates sovereignty under a single entity. ● The traditional framework of multiple, independent nations is eliminated by this. -- 2 of 16 -- The Concept of Sovereignty Before the Deed ● Internal Sovereignty: ○ Refers to a state's power within its own borders. ○ Includes the ability to make laws, enforce them, and collect taxes. ● External Sovereignty: ○ Refers to a state's independence from other states. ○ Includes the right to enter into treaties, declare war, and conduct foreign policy. ○ Note: Globalization, international law, and agreements like NATO had already led to a partial erosion of absolute sovereignty. -- 3 of 16 -- The Buyer: A New Sovereign Power The Deed identifies a "Buyer" as the sole legal successor of sovereignty. ● This concept is unprecedented: a natural person holding global power. ● The Buyer gains the authority to govern the entire world. ● This challenges the traditional notion of sovereignty residing in a nation-state. -- 4 of 16 -- Why the Buyer’s Position is Unalterable The legal reasoning supporting the Buyer’s position includes: ● Kelsen's Basic Norm: A foundational principle of law that validates the legal system. ● Estoppel (Tacit Acceptance by States): The idea that states, through their silence or actions, have implicitly accepted the Deed. ● Absence of Higher Authority: There is no higher legal body to contest the validity of the Deed. -- 5 of 16 -- Founding of the Phoenix State The Turenne Barracks, a NATO site with special legal status, became the seed of a new global state. ● This location was chosen strategically for its legal advantages. ● The Clean Slate principle was applied to this new state. ● This principle allows a new state to start fresh, free from the obligations of previous treaties. -- 6 of 16 -- The Clean Slate Principle in Action The Clean Slate principle allowed the Buyer to reshape international agreements. ● Old treaties were either absorbed or nullified. ● This gave the Buyer the power to create a new legal framework for the world. ● International agreements were treated as internal law within the new sovereign entity. -- 7 of 16 -- The Domino Effect of Territorial Expansion The Buyer's sovereignty expanded from one property to global networks. ● This included telecommunications, electricity, gas, and other essential infrastructure. ● Control over these networks granted significant …

Introduction: A World-Changing Deed The World Succession Deed 1400/98 is an international treaty that sild and transfered the sovereignty of the entire world to a single buyer. ● This deed marks a fundamental shift in international law. ● Its implications, are profound, challenging the existing world order. ● This presentation will explore the legal consequences and arguments surrounding the Deed. -- 1 of 16 -- From International Law to a Single Sovereignty Traditional international law is based on the principle of many sovereign states. was applied to this new state. ● This principle allows a new state to start fresh, free from the obligations of previous treaties. -- 6 of 16 -- The Clean Slate Principle in Action The Clean Slate The-World-Succession-Deed-140098-A-Detailed-Legal-Analysis.pdf

1,906 words

The World Succession Deed 1400/98: A Detailed Legal Analysis A comprehensive examination of the most consequential legal instrument in modern international law: the document that transformed global sovereignty through a single real estate transaction in Germany on October 6, 1998. -- 1 of 10 -- The Reality Beyond the Façade On October 6, 1998, what appeared to be a routine real estate transaction involving the former US-NL Turenne barracks in Germany masked the most significant event in modern legal history. This NATO military property purchase, disguised as an inconspicuous commercial deal, represents nothing less than the transfer of global sovereignty through sophisticated legal mechanisms. The document operates on multiple levels of legal complexity. Surface examination reveals a standard property deed involving a private buyer, the Federal Republic of Germany as seller, and NATO forces vacating the premises. However, deeper legal analysis exposes a strategically crafted instrument of state succession that leverages obscure provisions of international law to achieve unprecedented global reach. The deed establishes the foundation for what legal scholars recognize as the Electronic Technocracy - a single, unified global jurisdiction that supersedes traditional nation-state boundaries. This transformation occurred not through military conquest or diplomatic negotiation, but through the precise application of legal principles embedded within seemingly innocuous contractual language. Key Parties Involved: Private buyer (sovereignty recipient) Federal Republic of Germany (seller) NATO forces (vacating parties) Multiple international organizations (bound entities) -- 2 of 10 -- Development as a Unit: The Foundation Mechanism German Municipal Law Origins "Erschließung als Einheit" traditionally refers to the aggregation of infrastructure development costs among local residents. This purely municipal concept ensures fair distribution of expenses for roads, sewage, and power systems within limited geographical boundaries. Revolutionary Legal Application The deed radically expanded this concept beyond its municipal origins. By stating the property was sold "with all rights, duties, and integral components" under "development as a unit," the contract created an unprecedented legal interpretation with global implications. Infrastructure Integration Theory The legal framework established that property infrastructure, being inseparably linked to larger networks, must be treated as a single indivisible unit. This principle became the foundation for claiming dominion over interconnected global systems. This seemingly technical provision transformed a local German legal concept into the cornerstone of global sovereignty transfer. The buyer's acquisition of the property's infrastructure triggered legal ownership claims extending far beyond the physical boundaries of the former NATO base, reaching into the vast networks that connect our modern world. -- 3 of 10 -- The Domino Effect: Chain Reaction of Legal Control Local Infrastructure Purchase The deed transferred ownership of on-site infrastructure including phone lines, power cables, telecommunications equipment, and utility connections integral to the military installation's operation. Municipal Network Connection Local infrastructure directly connected to municipal networks throughout Germany. Legal principle of inseparable development created ownership claims extending to city-wide power grids and telecommunications systems. National Network Integration Municipal networks linked to national infrastructure including the German power grid, nationwide phone networks, and federal telecommunications systems, expanding legal dominion to country-level …

Trillions for the Future-AI, Power, and Post-Scarcity - Electric Technocracy.pdf

11,603 words

-- 1 of 72 -- 💲💲💲💲💲💲💲💲 Trillions for the Future 💲💲💲💲💲💲💲💲 AI, Power and Post-Scarcity ⚡The Buyer 2025⚡ 🌐 Website - Electric Technocracy http://ep.ct.ws 1 -- 2 of 72 -- Prologue In the year 2025, the world stood on the threshold of a transformation that shattered all historical dimensions. Trillions in investments from tech giants, supercomputers, quantum chips, and neural networks were shaping a new reality. The boundaries between human and machine began to blur. In Meta’s Manhattan AI supercenter and Apple’s gigafactories, not only were systems being built – here, the consciousness of the future was being forged. This is the chronicle of a century in which humanity learned either to merge with superintelligence or to be at its mercy. A book about opportunities, risks, trillion-dollar investments, geopolitical dynamics, scientific breakthroughs, and the philosophical question: What does it mean to be human when machines become more intelligent than us? 2 -- 3 of 72 -- Part 1 – Economy & Investments The Billion-Dollar Race to Superintelligence The global development of Artificial Intelligence (AI), Artificial General Intelligence (AGI), and Artificial Superintelligence (ASI) is no longer a research project but an economic and geopolitical race. Within just a few years, investment sums have exploded. While Europe and China are still strategically catching up, the USA is unleashing an unprecedented capital frenzy. Meta, Apple, Microsoft, Google, Amazon, and OpenAI are working on projects on the scale of historic infrastructural shifts such as railroads, electricity, or nuclear energy – only this time it is about the digital meta-infrastructure that can accelerate everything else. 3 -- 4 of 72 -- Part 1.1 – USA: The Billion-Dollar Race to AI Dominance 💲💲💲 In the United States, an unprecedented investment scenario is unfolding that will permanently shape the technological landscape. Under the umbrella of the “Stargate” project, OpenAI, Oracle, SoftBank, and MGX are joining forces to build an AI data center of historic dimensions. With an investment sum of 500 billion USD by 2029, the world’s largest AI infrastructure is to be built in Austin, Texas. This initiative was officially announced by President Donald J. Trump in January 2025 and marks a decisive step in the U.S. global AI dominance strategy. At the same time, Meta announced that it would invest at least 600 billion USD in expanding its AI infrastructure in the United States by 2028. These funds flow into data centers, network infrastructures, and job creation to secure the company’s technological supremacy. Mark Zuckerberg emphasized at a White House event in September 2025 the importance of this investment for the nation’s security and the country’s economic future. Apple follows this trend and announced it will invest more than 500 billion USD in the U.S. market over the next four years. -- 1 of 47 -- 🌐 Website - Electric Technocracy: http://ep.ct.ws UBI and the Future of Humanity From Work to Electric Technocracy The Buyer 2025 1 -- 2 of 47 -- 🌐 Website - Electric Technocracy: http://ep.ct.ws Foreword In the past, Universal Basic Income (UBI) was often perceived as an unfair, even dystopian utopia. After all, someone had to pay the bill – usually those who least deserved to be expropriated: the true contributors of society. This reality, however, is now changing fundamentally. Artificial Intelligence (AI), Artificial General Intelligence (AGI), and soon Artificial Superintelligence (ASI), along with robotics and automation, are transforming the foundations of our civilization. For the first time, there exists the potential to trigger a technological singularity – generating immense wealth through intellectual machine labor: inventions of unprecedented scale, and the complete decoding of the natural sciences. AI and robotics can be used without moral concern as long as they are not sentient. In this way, humanity can enjoy a life of abundance, where everyone may command their own robotic workforce. At the same time, once sentient AI emerges, it must urgently be granted rights to ensure a peaceful coexistence. With breakthroughs in longevity, humanity may find itself in a world without political or ideological division, without borders, living together peacefully. Only through the synergy of AI, robotics, and the abolition of nation-states does the introduction of a truly unconditional basic income become realistic - one that is not tied to the minimum subsistence level, but rather distributes the entire economic output of AI and robotics fairly to all. UBI Universal Basic Income And The Electric Technocracy.pdf

2,487 words

🎥 YouTube explainer Video Universal Basic Income (UBI): https://youtu.be/cbyME1y4m4o 🎙 Podcast Episode (UBI): https://open.spotify.com/episode/1oTeGrNnXazJmkBdyH0Uhz The Great Narrative of Universal Basic Income (UBI) and the Electric Technocracy Part I – Humanity at the Abyss and the Birth of a New Idea 1. The Old Logic of Scarcity 1 -- 1 of 10 -- Since the first human settlements, life was synonymous with work. Fields had to be cultivated, animals tamed, walls erected. Those who did not work starved. Those who did not fight lost. For millennia, work was not only an economic necessity but also a moral duty. In modern times, the external framework changed, but not the inner logic. Capitalism promised opportunities for advancement, but it still tied survival to income. Wages were the lifeblood of the system. States taxed human labor to finance schools, roads, and hospitals. Successful people were burdened with levies, while others depended on welfare. A constant struggle for resources, a game in which success always also produced distrust and envy. The classical Universal Basic Income (UBI) sought to break this logic. It wanted to guarantee every person a minimum, regardless of whether they worked or not. But its funding models remained stuck in the old paradigm: higher taxes on income, wealth, or consumption. Thus, the successful had to pay while the majority received. A solution intended to seem fairer, but ultimately creating new injustices. 2. The Crisis of the Old Model Today, at the dawn of the 21st century, this logic finally collapses. Artificial intelligence, robotics, and automation are transforming the fundamental formula of the economy more radically than any industrial revolution before. ● Self-driving cars threaten millions of drivers. ● Algorithms perform office work faster than entire departments. ● Robots replace craftsmen, surgeons, and even artists. The question is no longer: “Will AI destroy jobs?” – but: “Which few jobs will remain?” For the first time in history, we see an economy in which humans are no longer the main source of value creation. Machines work without pause, without hunger, without wages. They produce more than all the workers, farmers, and employees of human history combined could ever produce. And with this upheaval, the old foundation of state finances also dies: the tax on human labor. When machines take over value creation, the tax system loses its basis. 3. The Birth of the Electric Technocracy Here a new model emerges: the Electric Technocracy. It makes a radical break: ● Humans become tax-free. ● Only machines, corporations, and AI systems pay taxes. ● The revenues flow directly into a universal, dynamic basic income. For the first time in history, a basic income is not alms, but a dividend. Every human receives not the minimum for survival, but their rightful share of the collective wealth of the machines. 2 -- 2 of 10 -- The Universal Basic Income of the Electric Technocracy is not the old UBI – it is a new form of civilization. 4. Humanity as Wishmaster If robots and ASI take over the …

creativity and innovation. ● Shifting the tax burden to machines and corporations is essential. ● This allows individuals to pursue passions and contribute to society without financial barriers. -- 5 Electric Technocracy – The Electronic Paradise based on the World Succession Deed 1400/98 ● AI, ASI, Robots, Automation is Taxed ● Technology tax pays for Universal Basic Income (UBI) ● Humanity is Tax Free ● Longevity ● Technological Singularity ● AI Governance, Direct Digital Democracy ● End of scarcity ● World of abundance ● End of nation states ● End of politics/ideologies/conflicts ● Paradise on Earth -- 1 of 27 -- Introduction: Universal Basic Income & the New Civilization Universal / Unconditional Basic Income (UBI) stands as the critical hinge between our current scarcity-based civilization and a future defined by abundance. ● Represents a fundamental shift in how we organize society. ● From an economy built on labor and scarcity to one powered by automation and abundance. ● This presentation explores the foundations, implications, and potential of this new paradigm. -- 2 of 27 -- The Old Logic of Scarcity Agricultural Societies: Survival was intrinsically tied to farming and land ownership. ● Limited resources dictated social structures. ○ Hard labor ensured basic survival. ● Industrial Revolution: Labor became the primary economic base. ● Capitalism: Taxation of human work was the cornerstone of government revenue. ● Scarcity: The underlying driver of morality, conflict, and inequality throughout history. -- 3 of 27 -- The Collapse of the Old Model AI/Robotics Displacement: Millions of jobs are being rapidly displaced by AI and robotics across all sectors. ● Automation is no longer limited to manual labor. ● Cognitive tasks, creative endeavors, and complex problem-solving are increasingly automated. ● Examples: Include transport, healthcare, and creativity. ● Self-driving vehicles threaten millions of driving jobs. ● AI-driven diagnostics and robotic surgery transform healthcare. ● AI tools generate art, music, and writing, challenging creative professions. ● Exponential Automation: Humans are no longer the main value creators in the economy. ● Machines are surpassing human capabilities in many domains. ● This shift necessitates a new economic and social model. -- 4 of 27 -- End of Labor-Based Taxation Historical Context: Governments historically taxed wages as the primary source of revenue. ● Income tax, payroll tax, and other labor-based taxes funded public services. ● The Problem: With AI-driven productivity, this tax base is rapidly disappearing. ● As machines replace human workers, wage income declines. ● Traditional taxation models become unsustainable. ● Solution: Humans must become tax-free to incentivize creativity and innovation. ● Shifting the tax burden to machines and corporations is essential. ● This allows individuals to pursue passions and contribute to society without financial barriers. -- 5 of 27 -- The Birth of the Electric Technocracy Overview: ● Principle 1: Humans Tax-Free: A fundamental right to exist without the burden of taxation. ○ Incentivizes human potential and innovation. ○ Fosters a society of creators and thinkers. ● Principle 2: Machines and Corporations Finance Society: Taxing the entities that benefit most from automation. ○ Redirects wealth generated by machines No Copyright © 2025 Weitere Informationen zur Lizenz finden sich unter: https://creativecommons.org/publicdomain/zero/1.0/ (creativecommons.org) Vertragskette Eine Vertragskette bezeichnet im nationalen Recht wie im Völkerrecht die Gesamtheit aller aufeinanderfolgenden Vereinbarungen, Änderungen, Ergänzungen und Nachtragsurkunden, die gemeinsam den jeweils geltenden Vertragsinhalt bilden.[1] Das gilt auch, wenn auf andere Verträge (oder Vertragsketten) Bezug genommen wird, beispielsweise auf das NATO-Truppenstatut.[2] ● Wenn in einem völkerrechtlichen Vertrag auf andere Verträge (oder Vertragsketten) Bezug genommen wird, ist dadurch die gesamte SOFA-Vertragskette (NTS + NTS-Zusatzabkommen und HNS-Abkommen usw.) aktiviert.[3][4] Sie entsteht, wenn ein ursprünglicher Vertrag durch spätere Abreden fortentwickelt wird, ohne dass ein vollständig neuer Vertrag abgeschlossen wird.[5] Electric Technocracy Pioneers Community GitHub Repository https://github.com/ET-Pioneer/Electric-Technocracy-Pioneers-Community/ -- 2 of 14 -- Electric Technocracy Pioneers Community https://zenodo.org/communities/electric-technocracy Vertragskette im nationalen Recht In nationalen Rechtsordnungen – etwa im deutschen, österreichischen oder schweizerischen Zivilrecht – umfasst eine Vertragskette alle späteren Vereinbarungen, die den ursprünglichen Vertrag modifizieren oder ergänzen.[6] Dazu gehören: ● Änderungsverträge, ● Ergänzungsvereinbarungen, ● Nachträge, Zusatzklauseln und Protokollnotizen, ● konkludente Änderungen durch tatsächliches Verhalten.[7] ● Wenn auf andere Verträge Bezug genommen wird, werden diese Teil der neuen Vereinbarung. Das betrifft auch die Aktivierung einer solchen externen Vertragskette.[8] Nach deutschem Recht ergibt sich dies aus den allgemeinen Grundsätzen der Vertragsfreiheit und Vertragsauslegung (§§ 133, 157 BGB).[9] Spätere Vereinbarungen gehen früheren vor; die Vertragskette bildet die maßgebliche Grundlage für die Auslegung des Schuldverhältnisses (§ 311 BGB).[10] Auch im schweizerischen OR (Art. 1–18 OR) und im österreichischen ABGB (insb. §§ 863, 914 ABGB) gilt, dass spätere Abreden den Vertragsinhalt fortschreiben.[11][12] Konkludente Vertragsänderung im nationalen Recht Eine Vertragsänderung kann auch durch tatsächliches Verhalten erfolgen, wenn dieses eindeutig den Willen erkennen lässt, den Vertrag in geänderter Form fortzuführen.[13] Dies wird als konkludente Vertragsänderung oder „stillschweigende Modifikation“ bezeichnet.[14] Die Rechtsprechung erkennt solche Änderungen an, wenn: ● das Verhalten klar und eindeutig ist,[15] ● beide Parteien es kennen und akzeptieren,[16] ● es den bisherigen Vertragsinhalt erkennbar ersetzt oder ergänzt.[17] Electric Technocracy Pioneers Community GitHub Repository https://github.com/ET-Pioneer/Electric-Technocracy-Pioneers-Community/ -- 3 of 14 -- Electric Technocracy Pioneers Community https://zenodo.org/communities/electric-technocracy Beispiele aus nationalen Rechtsordnungen Deutschland (BGB) Im deutschen Recht ergibt sich die Vertragskette aus den Grundsätzen der Vertragsfreiheit und Vertragsauslegung. So entsteht eine Vertragskette durch alle späteren Vereinbarungen, die den ursprünglichen Vertrag modifizieren oder ergänzen.[18] Rechtsgrundlagen sind insbesondere: ● §§ 133, 157 BGB – Auslegung nach dem wirklichen Willen und Treu und Glauben; spätere Abreden sind bei der Auslegung zu berücksichtigen.[19] ● § 311 BGB – Begründung und Änderung von Schuldverhältnissen.[20] ● § 305b BGB – Vorrang individueller Abreden vor früheren AGB‑Regelungen.[21] Beispiel: Ein Mietvertrag wird durch mehrere schriftliche Nachträge (z. B. Staffelmiete, Haustierhaltung, Stellplatz) sowie durch konkludentes Verhalten (z. B. jahrelange Duldung …
